 ฒฐ ฑฐฑ฿ ฿ฐ ฐฑ฿฿฿฿฿฿ฒ฿ฒ฿฿฿ฒ฿฿ ฿ฑฒฒ ฿ฒ฿฿฿฿฿ ฿ฑ ฒ
 ฒ  ฐ฿ฐฑ฿ฐฑฒ ฿฿ฐ฿฿฿ฐฑฒ ฿ฑฒฐ฿ฐฑฒฐฑ฿ ฒ  ฐฑฒ ฐฑฒฑฒ฿฿
 ฒ  ฐฐฑ  ฐฑ฿ฐฑ฿ฐฑ฿฿ ฐฐฑ ฿ฐฒ฿ ฐฑ ฐ฿ฐฑฐฑ฿ฐฑ฿฿ฐฑ ฐฐฒ
 ฒ ฐฐฐฐ    ฐ ฐ ฐฑ ฐ฿ฐฒฒฐฐ ฐ฿ฐ ฐ ฐฐฑ ฿฿   ฐ  ฐ ฒ
 ฒ ฑฐ ฐ ฒฐฐฑฐฑ฿ ฐฑ฿฿ฒ ฐฒฒ ฐ ฐ฿ฐ ฐฐฑ฿ ฿฿ ฐ ฐฒ
 ฐ ฐฐ ฿฿ฐฐ฿  ฐ ฿ฐฐ฿฿ ฿ ฐ฿ฒ ฐ ฿฿ฐฐ฿฿ฐ฿ ฿ฐ฿ฐฒ
  ฿฿  ฿  ฿   


 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : <Undisclosed>        บ
 บ    Subject  : Piracy                    Affiliation : Apogee               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Software companies had a hard time when games were released on      บ
 บ        diskettes since diskettes can easily be copied.  However, most      บ
 บ        companies currently release games on CD-Rom.  Since it is often     บ
 บ        difficult to pirate a game that is 650 megabytes, do software       บ
 บ        companies feel that CD-Rom has deterred piracy?                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : That depends on what is on the CD-Rom.  If a game is 20 megabytes,  บ
 บ        and it's on a CD, it's just as easy to pirate it.  CD's are also    บ
 บ        cheaper to produce and floppies, and last longer.  If someone is    บ
 บ        going to steal a computer program, they'll steal it no matter what  บ
 บ        format it's on.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I assume Apogee knows that the final registered version of Duke     บ
 บ        Nukem 3D will be released on the internet BEFORE it hits stores.    บ
 บ        Ironically, it will most likely be uploaded to the internet and     บ
 บ        given to a games pirate group by an Apogee insider.  Will Apogee    บ
 บ        assume preventive measures in the future so that Apogee software    บ
 บ        is not pirated?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : As long as human beings are involved, there will always be people   บ
 บ        who will want to steal a computer program.  It's human nature.  No  บ
 บ        matter what you do, someone will steal your program.  Period.       บ
 บ        There's ultimately nothing you can do if someone really wants to    บ
 บ        steal your program.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you're saying that Apogee KNOWS people pirate their software     บ
 บ        and is doing nothing to prevent it because Apogee feels that        บ
 บ        stealing is human nature?                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : I'm saying that every computer software programmer knows people     บ
 บ        pirate their software.  There is no such thing as a method of       บ
 บ        protection that can totally prevent your software from being        บ
 บ        stolen.  I'm not saying that Apogee does nothing.  I'm saying that  บ
 บ        you're naive to think you can totally protect your software.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Some companies DO find a way to make sure their software is         บ
 บ        IMPOSSIBLE to pirate on the internet.  They make their games        บ
 บ        ridiculously LARGE.  For example, Phantasmagoria was released on    บ
 บ        seven CDs, will Apogee take that route in the future by making      บ
 บ        games that often take up many CDs?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : I doubt that.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : For example, ALL games that include MacroMedia are IMPOSSIBLE to    บ
 บ        pirate on the internet due to their extensive size, and are thus,   บ
 บ        HARDLY ever pirated.  However, those games that are HARDLY pirated  บ
 บ        do not sell as well as games that ARE pirated.  Why are software    บ
 บ        companies turning to MacroMedia, a form of programming that         บ
 บ        requires HALF the usual programming time and are nearly pirate      บ
 บ        free?                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : If you are inferring that huge CD-Rom games are not pirated, then   บ
 บ        you're wrong.  Haven't you heard of CD-Rom burners?  These things   บ
 บ        are below $1000, and they'll go much lower soon.  The CD-Rom is     บ
 บ        *NOT* protection from copying software anymore, and will be less    บ
 บ        so in the future.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You can copy a huge game from CD to CD, but you cannot upload or    บ
 บ        download them from underground bulletin boards because it would     บ
 บ        take a person about 1 week to download a game on a 33.6kb/s         บ
 บ        US Robotics Modem.  Is that not true?                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : Yeah, but if you think that's the only avenue of piracy, you're     บ
 บ        not seeing everything.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is the main avenue of piracy?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : What do you think it is?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I go over my friend's house and we lend each other SNES games, and  บ
 บ        sometimes PC games too.  I've only copied like 3 games, and I       บ
 บ        guess a lot of my friends also do what I do, so it must add up.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : The internet is the main avenue of trading, and countries outside   บ
 บ        of the United States pose a big problem too.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : The internet?  People pirate on the internet?  So... ya got any     บ
 บ        cool sitez, d00d?                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Method               บ
 บ    Subject  : Couriers on Conquest      Affiliation : COC President        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is Couriers on Conquest?  I assume it's a courier group, but   บ
 บ        what will make it different from all the other courier groups that  บ
 บ        pop up each week?                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : Couriers on Conquest came up from a couple of places.  When DiC     บ
 บ        decided to merge with some no name group, a lot of DiC members did  บ
 บ        not like it so we decided to go run DiC ourselves, but the          บ
 บ        President of DiC didn't like the idea.  Then, a couple local        บ
 บ        friends of mine decided we wanted to run a local courier group for  บ
 บ        the time being; and if it got a good response, then we would take   บ
 บ        it to the NET.  I had a local sysop make up a quick application     บ
 บ        generator and we had a good response of eager couriers,             บ
 บ        programmers, artists, and distribution sites.  We then decided to   บ
 บ        bring it to the NET and so far, we haven't had a bad response.  We  บ
 บ        are different because we aren't out there to get the best name or   บ
 บ        trade the fastest.  We just want to get out there and have some     บ
 บ        fun trying to courier.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Have you experienced any trouble with past DiC members that merged  บ
 บ        with that no name group?  Do any of them hold grudges against you   บ
 บ        or COC?  If so, what have they done?                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : Actually, a day later, the President took a lot of our advice and   บ
 บ        pulled out of the merge, and then DiC fell apart, but now it's      บ
 บ        back under new the new President, Blackened.  I hope they do        บ
 บ        better.  I have never really had a problem with any of the past or  บ
 บ        present DiC members.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What must one do to become a COC member?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : Couriers need to have internet accounts so they can access IRC      บ
 บ        and FTP.  There are really no requirements for distribution sites.  บ
 บ        We are really out to have fun.  If you apply, there's a 99% chance  บ
 บ        you'll get in the group.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Many other groups have proven success by being very selective and   บ
 บ        letting very FEW people in the group.  Why and how do you feel      บ
 บ        that letting in 99% of all applicants will in turn benefit COC?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : I believe in giving everyone a chance to prove themselves, in a     บ
 บ        couple weeks I will cut whoever is slacking.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is COC planning to courier and release in the future since many     บ
 บ        new courier groups do so?                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : We are currently strictly couriering, but may be, this is a big     บ
 บ        may be, if we do succeed in the future, we might release as well    บ
 บ        as courier.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you connect couriering power of a group with how well they can   บ
 บ        release?  The big groups such as RiSC/RTS/MC never release warez.   บ
 บ        Do you think that perhaps a courier group that DOES release might   บ
 บ        not be as good as a courier group that does NOT?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : I see it as, a courier group that does release has more problems    บ
 บ        and is more disorganized because the group needs to worry about     บ
 บ        dupes and fakes.  I think that is why more courier groups go down,  บ
 บ        but courier groups that don't release don't have to worry about     บ
 บ        dupes and fakes and just have to stay organized and courier.  That  บ
 บ        is why I feel that there is a higher chance of COC staying alive    บ
 บ        if we don't release.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Where did you come up with the name COC?  It sounds like a person   บ
 บ        sucking on a cock, isn't that a bad name for the group?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : I know.  I have heard all the little names that COC could stand     บ
 บ        for.  I really don't know.  I thought of conquest and put it all    บ
 บ        together and didn't really think about the initials of the group    บ
 บ        until someone pointed it out to me.  It doesn't really seem to be   บ
 บ        bringing the group down, and I don't think it really matters what   บ
 บ        the name of the group is, as long as we all stay together and well  บ
 บ        organized.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Are there any older courier groups that you model after?            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : Well, there are some courier groups that just go up to get warez    บ
 บ        and then there are REAL courier groups that have made a impression  บ
 บ        on everyone.  I personally like fATE, RiSC, MindCrash, and Legacy.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Legacy is a games group, but anyways, do you feel that your past    บ
 บ        experience in DiC has proved beneficial in helping you run COC?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : I saw in DiC that if you weren't organized, you wouldn't make it    บ
 บ        anywhere in the scene.  DiC taught me to keep my group organized    บ
 บ        and tight.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Cybernetic           บ
 บ    Subject  : Distinct                  Affiliation : Ex-DTC Member        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is your current position in Distinct?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  CYB : Since Distinct broke up, I'm not so sure.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What happened on the night of January 29 in #Distinct?  Why did     บ
 บ        Distinct break up, and why did it start up again so soon after it   บ
 บ        died?                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  CYB : It all started when Bullet Wound was kicked from Distinct.  Then,   บ
 บ        after school today, I came home to find that our channel had been   บ
 บ        taken over.  I got the channel back, and within 5 minutes, Violent  บ
 บ        (Distinct High Council) came into #Distinct and changed the         บ
 บ        channel topic to :                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ            'GET THE FUCK OUT, DISTINCT IS DEAD'                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ        Later this evening, Weed (Distinct Senior) came into #Distinct and  บ
 บ        changed topic to :                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ            Distinct, Still Trading!                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ        I'm not really sure if Weed wants to start it back up or not, but   บ
 บ        I do belive that two seniors, Axxis and Mystic One left and that    บ
 บ        Violent and Vertigox are gone.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : There seems to be a power struggle between Weed and Vertigox.       บ
 บ        While both Weed and Vertigox were still in Distinct back when it    บ
 บ        was still officially running, did you feel that there were strong   บ
 บ        conflicts between the two?                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  CYB : I didn't see a conflict, but it always seemed as if they weren't    บ
 บ        so close and it seemed to me that Weed would rather he be in        บ
 บ        charge.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you feel that Weed plotted the death of Distinct so he could     บ
 บ        run it after Vertigox and Violent left?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  CYB : No, i don't think it was Weed's idea to kill Distinct.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you feel that Distinct will be better off now that Vertigox and  บ
 บ        Violent are NOT running the group?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  CYB : Better, yes, in a way.  Wouldn't the government run better with a   บ
 บ        Vice President that helped the President?  The question is, will    บ
 บ        Distinct live on in order for that to happen.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You stated earlier that the fall of Distinct first started when     บ
 บ        Bullet Wound was kicked out of Distinct; why was he kicked out?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  CYB : Vertigox mass deoped everyone, but since Bullet Wound's script      บ
 บ        automatically kickbans anyone that tries to mass deop, Vertigox     บ
 บ        got really pissed when he was kickbanned out of the channel.  In    บ
 บ        turn, Vertigox kicked Bullet Wound out of Distinct.  Since Bullet   บ
 บ        Wound was a senior courier, the group fell part and killed itself   บ
 บ        in his absence.  Therefore, Vertigox and Violent decided to kill    บ
 บ        Distinct before it drove itself right into the ground.  Vertigox    บ
 บ        didn't want it to end like that, so he killed the group.  We could  บ
 บ        have been a great competitive group.                                บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What was your position in the former Distinct?  Did you feel that   บ

 บ        several high caliber sites for the group.  We had an opportunity    บ
 บ        to make the group into something special.  Unfortunately the        บ
 บ        leadership was not interested in the growth and betterment of the   บ
 บ        group.  A group must be made up of members working toward a common  บ

 บ        leadership did not mind if the couriers couriered 2-3 day warez     บ

 บ        to fight for almost a week just to get the damn channel '+i'.  He   บ
 บ        fought the high council on this point.  He has been around for a    บ
 บ        long time and he knew that keeping the channel '-i' was a mistake.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Raistlindr           บ
 บ    Subject  : fATE                      Affiliation : Ex-fATE Member       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The following is a reinterview with Raistlindr made in order to clear     บ
 บ  some misconceptions :                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why were you kicked out of fATE?                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : I told Anti Derivative when I spoke with him that I was no longer   บ
 บ        in fATE and I thought he understood that.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why did you tell him you were no longer in fATE?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : For a few reasons, 1. The fact that Anti Derivative and god were    บ
 บ        never online to take care of any problems.  2. LeoDLioN is one of   บ
 บ        the most childish and infantile people I know on the net.  3. The   บ
 บ        fact that most of the fATE people were not doing anything.  4. The  บ
 บ        fact that if there was ever a problem, they would just try to kick  บ
 บ        you out of the channel, and did not allow you to defend yourself.   บ
 บ        Those are the main reasons.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : If Anti Derivative and god were not online to take care of          บ
 บ        problems, then who did to help accomplish things?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : In theory, the other seniors did, and that was one of the main      บ
 บ        problems, was the fact that much of it didn't get taken care of.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why do you feel that LeoDLioN is childish and infantile?  He is     บ
 บ        married and has kids.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : That does not matter and is not what I meant.  His attitude and     บ
 บ        how he reacts to other people.  For instance, if he has a problem   บ
 บ        with someone instead of speaking to them rationally or allowing     บ
 บ        them to defend themselves he will just try and kick them out of     บ
 บ        the channel anytime there has been a problem with him.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Has he ever done anything personally to you that would turn you     บ
 บ        off?                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : And when I have stopped the escalation of the problem, he would     บ
 บ        always start up again.  And, yes, he has done a lot to me.  When I  บ
 บ        was still in fATE, he took me off the bots and banned me from       บ
 บ        #fATE because he realized that I was correct and that he could not  บ
 บ        defend his actions, so rather than admit he was wrong or try and    บ
 บ        solve any problems, he just tried to ban me. As long as I was       บ
 บ        still in fATE, as I was, I should not be taken off the bots, much   บ
 บ        less banned from them.  That is just one example of how childish    บ
 บ        he acts.  He did not like the fact that he felt he could question   บ
 บ        what I stated and basically stated I was lying and did not like     บ
 บ        the fact that when he did this, I would defend myself and           บ
 บ        question his actions.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What did you state?                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : Well, I am a very good "warez-encyclopedia".  I know all the files  บ
 บ        and what was out and when, and back then I was not currently in     บ
 บ        DMN (Demolition) and a DMN senior came into the channel and asked   บ
 บ        me directly a question about something DMN was planning on          บ
 บ        releasing and I stated that the program in question was not out as  บ
 บ        of yet.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : To dupe check?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : Yes, to dupe check it.  Then LeoDLioN decided to insert himself in  บ
 บ        the conversation and started ordering me to go log off the NET and  บ
 บ        call Park Central for the files.  I had stated that was not         บ
 บ        necessary as I knew it was not out.  I asked the DMN senior who     บ
 บ        had asked me the question and he stated to me that my answer was    บ
 บ        quite sufficient and the fact that I stated it was enough for him   บ
 บ        to believe it.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So do you belive that LeoDLioN, Anti Derivate, and god were bad     บ
 บ        for fATE, because they either did nothing, or are immature?         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : Well, I believe that LeoDLioN is bad for the group and that Anti    บ
 บ        Derivative and god can't be good for it as they are not in enough   บ
 บ        to take care of their duties.  I basically feel that LeoDLioN is    บ
 บ        much too infantile and childish to be more of an asset to a group   บ
 บ        than a hindrance.  For me at least, the main problem was that he    บ
 บ        was very egotistical and felt that his opinions could not be        บ
 บ        questioned, yet still felt that he could question others.  My main  บ
 บ        problem with him was that he inserted himself in a conversation     บ
 บ        that did not involve him and then proceeded to take offense when I  บ
 บ        questioned what he stated because he questioned what I stated.  I   บ
 บ        did not at the time harbor any bad feelings toward god or Anti      บ
 บ        Derivative, but the fact that I tried for over 2 weeks to get in    บ
 บ        touch with one of them to resolve this and neither of them were     บ
 บ        ever in did not help my disposition towards fATE.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Raw Toxic                 Interviewee : Majorr               บ
 บ    Subject  : SODOM                     Affiliation : SDM Senior           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is SODOM?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : SODOM is a warez group organized in Russia.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Most of us have never heard of SODOM, how long has SODOM been in    บ
 บ        existence?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : SODOM has been around for a year now, a little less or a little     บ
 บ        more, give or take.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Are warez a big thing in Russia as in comparsion to the United      บ
 บ        States?                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : The warez scene in Russia is about if not equal to the one in the   บ
 บ        United States.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are some of SODOM's goals?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : Our main goal is to monopolize the Russian warez market.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : D0D's slogan is `Warez Bears from Russia'.  Is D0D competition for  บ
 บ        SODOM?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : Actually D0D only has about 3 members who are actually from         บ
 บ        Russia; so their slogan doesn't really fit the entire group.  D0D   บ
 บ        is too large to be a Russian warez group.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is your opinion of the warez scene?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : There's too much worthless crap being released, half of it doesn't  บ
 บ        work, the other half is just useless.  SODOM refuses to courier     บ
 บ        such garbage.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Has the KGB been cutting down on warez in Russia?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : No.  Microsoft has tried to grab some CD retailers, but it was a    บ
 บ        one-time deal.  They failed against the Russian bears!  However,    บ
 บ        there are some laws concerning copyrights in Russia, but they       บ
 บ        don't work at all.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Has SODOM experienced any internal problems?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : No, we don't have many problems for two reasons, we are all in      บ
 บ        SODOM for a common goal, and half of us know each other on a        บ
 บ        personal level.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What do you see in SODOM's future?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : I see that while we are expanding in Russia, we will also grow      บ
 บ        outside of Russia.  We would like to keep more than half of our     บ
 บ        group Russian though.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How does SODOM handle slackers?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : We just kick them out of the group.  It's easy to do it, every      บ
 บ        member in SODOM must contribute something useful.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How is the Russian warez scene different from the American warez    บ
 บ        scene?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : There really aren't any groups in Russia.  SODOM is the only        บ
 บ        serious warez group in Russia.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Has the Russian scene grown considerably due to SODOM?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : Of course not, we aren't the first group in the Russian scene,      บ
 บ        there was DOD before SODOM.  We just want to be the greatest        บ
 บ        Russian group ever.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How are you going to make SODOM the greatest Russian group ever?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : SODOM is going to unite all the guys in Russia who are able to do   บ
 บ        something and we are going to work in that direction.  We have      บ
 บ        many former D0D members joining SODOM so we have a good start.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When you mentioned formerr D0D members, did they give up D0D to     บ
 บ        join SODOM?                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : No, they were kicked out by Jimmy Jamez and SODOM was willing to    บ
 บ        let them in.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How do you say 'warez' in Russian?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : Waresi                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Super Hacker         บ
 บ    Subject  : The Hardened Criminals    Affiliation : THC President        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What sets THC apart from other courier groups?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : Well, there are many things.  One is the name.  As you can see,     บ
 บ        the name is not related nor does it sound like a couriering group.  บ
 บ        It sounds more like bunch of criminals doing illegal activities.    บ
 บ        GUESS WHAT, we are all doing this, and we are all criminals.  The   บ
 บ        main reason why the group is different and set APART from other     บ
 บ        couriering groups is that members in our group are dedicated.  We   บ
 บ        all work in groups and we all have a common goal.  We are here to   บ
 บ        have fun and to help out the warez scene to the best of our         บ
 บ        abilities.  Like we say  "HERO'S COME AND GO, BUT CRIMINALS NEVER   บ
 บ        DIE" SO BANNNNNNNNNG, we are here to stay.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are the minimum requirements for an accepted THC applicant?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : THC looks for dedication, time, and leadership skills in new        บ
 บ        applicants.  We are not like other groups in that we do not ask a   บ
 บ        member to be on IRC 24 hours a day trading.  Everybody has a life   บ
 บ        and we as a group want people to contribute whatever time they can  บ
 บ        and expect only 100% dedication.  If the new member can only        บ
 บ        contribute 5 hours a day trading, then that's cool as long as he    บ
 บ        puts 100% in that 5 hours.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you feel that people might become lazy under that philosphy?     บ
 บ        Is it working for THC so far?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : THC has been working well under our current philosophy.  People     บ
 บ        are not becoming lazy but are becoming more active.  People who     บ
 บ        courier for 5 hours or so are now couriering 10 hours.  I don't     บ
 บ        know how but they are.  They even come up with new ideas of making  บ
 บ        the group more effective, so our philosophy is definitely working.  บ
 บ        We also have members from other groups joining THC because they     บ
 บ        say groups like fATE, RTS, and MOTiV8 require more time.  So the    บ
 บ        facts and answers are right in front of us.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you feel that THC's philosphy will make it one of the BEST       บ
 บ        courier groups in the scene in the not too distant future?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : Yes, I believe that the THC philosophy will make us one of the      บ
 บ        best groups in the near future.  We have just started and we are    บ
 บ        doing well.  I did not expect that but with hard work and           บ
 บ        dedication we are doing really well.  One good thing I really       บ
 บ        enjoyed is that other courier groups don't bug us or do the usual   บ
 บ        CHANNEL TAKEOVERS.  I suppose those things only happen to release   บ
 บ        groups.  Our future plans are not only to accept couriers but to    บ
 บ        accept suppliers as well.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Since THC will be accepting suppliers, will it be releasing under   บ
 บ        a separate name or under THC?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : A branch of THC will release and the other good part will be that   บ
 บ        we can spread our own releases.  Like I said before, we are here    บ
 บ        to contribute toward the warez scene and are giving 100%.  If       บ
 บ        members can supply us with warez, then why not supply and courier   บ
 บ        together.  We can have the best of both worlds.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : THC sounds an awful lot like THG - The Humble Guys.  Did they in    บ
 บ        any way inspire the name THC?  Do members of THC look up to THG as  บ
 บ        models?  I remember memorizing it as an acronym so I could get on   บ
 บ        some lame one node board.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : Well, if you look at the letters THC, you would notice that if you  บ
 บ        flip flop the "T" and the "H", you'd get the name HTC as well; and  บ
 บ        like you said, it can also be flip flopped to form THG.  When I     บ
 บ        first started out in the scene, we were called TGP (Tokyo Ghetto    บ
 บ        Pussy).  We couriered and then changed our name to PWC (Pirate      บ
 บ        Without Cause), but we didn't like it.  The Humble Guys in a way    บ
 บ        did inspire us and so did other groups like PTW, DTC, and HTC.      บ
 บ        We took all the concepts and good parts of all those groups and     บ
 บ        formed THC.  We took all the good parts from each group and made a  บ
 บ        new group with a new look and style.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is THC best at internet or board couriering?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : We are best at board couriering.  The reason for this is that we    บ
 บ        have sysops from many areas.  We asked them to get us one of their  บ
 บ        users from their board who can call internet and get warez off our  บ
 บ        sites.  Using this method, we spread to our boards much faster.     บ
 บ        The users ftp to the sites, they leech 0-1 hour warez and then      บ
 บ        upload it to their assigned board.  The sysops can easily keep      บ
 บ        track of that because the sysop of the boards are all members of    บ
 บ        THC.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is THC's policy on double tagging?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : What is double tagging?                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do THC couriers tag files they help spread?                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : Yes, we put our NFO file in it.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Throughout these past 11 issues, Reality Check Network has received a     บ
 บ  great amount of user response.  The RCN staff has decided to publish      บ
 บ  these comments, whether supportive or destructive.  We would like to      บ
 บ  encourage our readers to continue to voice their opinions, and we would   บ
 บ  like to thank all the readers that have done so up until now.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN/Trite,                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First of all, thank you for your kind words about MALiCE, however as  บ
 บ  one of the leaders of MALiCE, I feel I have to address several issues     บ
 บ  your article mentioned about the group.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Group Interfacing and Relations -                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      MALiCE has no quarrels with other couriering groups, be it RiSC,      บ
 บ  Everlast, RTS, fATE, or any other.  May I re-iterate the policy of        บ
 บ  MALiCE, which may I add is written in our constitution.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  - MALiCE will not or shall not tolerate its own members slating or        บ
 บ    rubbishing other groups in public, on the boards, or on the net.  Such  บ
 บ    behavior is completely inappropriate.  MALiCE was formed for fun and    บ
 บ    certainly not for having egotrips or forms of bullshit.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I do admit in the early days of MALiCE's reformation, we did have     บ
 บ  problems with other groups, however such problems have been ironed out,   บ
 บ  and we extend our respect equally to all other groups.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  - May I add the channel big-headedness is not "might just be a tad out    บ
 บ    of date" but IT IS, by over 2 months.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  - Your presentation of our channel policy is untrue and is not based on   บ
 บ    true facts, but I would like to know where you received your            บ
 บ    information concerning our channel policy.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      However I would like to present the real policy of MALiCE based on    บ
 บ  facts.  MALiCE channel policy strictly states, people who get OPPED in    บ
 บ  the channel must be a member of the MALiCE team, any other ops must be    บ
 บ  approved by the leaders and this is only given out under SPECIAL          บ
 บ  circumstances.  People outside the group, with the exception of PWA,      บ
 บ  DARIUS, Rebels, AFL, Pinnacle, and/or friends of MALiCE may get invited,  บ
 บ  will not have ops, but rather +v.  This provides a harmonious and         บ
 บ  working relationship with the other groups, and may I add, the other      บ
 บ  groups extend the same invitation to MALiCE members as they visit their   บ
 บ  respective channels.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Finally, people who wish to join MALiCE may be invited to the         บ
 บ  channel but at the Council or Leader's discretion.  This is the MALiCE    บ
 บ  channel policy, and as you can see it clearly shows your statement about  บ
 บ  non-invitations to outsiders to be untrue and unfounded.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Publicity?  Well, publicity is not one of our main objectives,        บ
 บ  however, MALiCE's main objectives are :                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  - To have fun and a damn good time in what we do.                         บ
 บ  - To support our boards and our sites well.                               บ
 บ  - Spread the warez of the release groups (this extends to all groups be   บ
 บ    it the ones we courier for or not), on the boards (MALiCE and NON       บ
 บ    MALiCE included) and on the net sites (MALiCE and NON MALiCE included)  บ
 บ    and provide the release groups that we courier for officially, support  บ
 บ    on their major boards and sites.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      MALiCE does welcome publicity for itself only by achieving its        บ
 บ  defined objectives.  To gain publicity by inviting any John Doe on IRC    บ
 บ  is not our way of working, I'm afraid.  Lastly, to gain publicity as an   บ
 บ  individual objective is certainly not considered.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  "They do all recruiting by word-of-mouth which is not too bad, but not    บ
 บ   too good practice for a long lasting courier group."                     บ
 บ                                               - Trite (RCN #10, Articles)  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      May I ask you to justify your source for the above statement in your  บ
 บ  article?  We certainly do not do our recruiting by word-of-mouth, I have  บ
 บ  no idea where you got this notion from, but I will state it is untrue     บ
 บ  and unfounded.  We do our recruiting based on these attributes :          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  - The applicant would benefit MALiCE in helping achieve our goals and     บ
 บ    MALiCE can provide support for the applicant, to establish a two-way    บ
 บ    working relationship.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  - The applicant has a proven track record on the boards and/or the net    บ
 บ    and/or has been recommended to us by our other sources.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Once council and/or leaders have ascertained the applicant is suitable    บ
 บ  for membership we usually place the applicant on a two week trial         บ
 บ  period, which allows the applicant and MALiCE to determine whether it is  บ
 บ  the right choice for both respective parties.  Overall this policy has    บ
 บ  provided us with loyal and hardworking members, occasionally it has not,  บ
 บ  but it has been a tried and tested method, and we shall not be changing   บ
 บ  our recruiting policy in the near future.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ               Aslan - MALiCE Leader / RAZOR 1911 / DARiUS / PiNNACLE       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : <Undisclosed>        บ
 บ    Subject  : Piracy                    Affiliation : Apogee               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Software companies had a hard time when games were released on      บ
 บ        diskettes since diskettes can easily be copied.  However, most      บ
 บ        companies currently release games on CD-Rom.  Since it is often     บ
 บ        difficult to pirate a game that is 650 megabytes, do software       บ
 บ        companies feel that CD-Rom has deterred piracy?                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : That depends on what is on the CD-Rom.  If a game is 20 megabytes,  บ
 บ        and it's on a CD, it's just as easy to pirate it.  CD's are also    บ
 บ        cheaper to produce and floppies, and last longer.  If someone is    บ
 บ        going to steal a computer program, they'll steal it no matter what  บ
 บ        format it's on.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I assume Apogee knows that the final registered version of Duke     บ
 บ        Nukem 3D will be released on the internet BEFORE it hits stores.    บ
 บ        Ironically, it will most likely be uploaded to the internet and     บ
 บ        given to a games pirate group by an Apogee insider.  Will Apogee    บ
 บ        assume preventive measures in the future so that Apogee software    บ
 บ        is not pirated?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : As long as human beings are involved, there will always be people   บ
 บ        who will want to steal a computer program.  It's human nature.  No  บ
 บ        matter what you do, someone will steal your program.  Period.       บ
 บ        There's ultimately nothing you can do if someone really wants to    บ
 บ        steal your program.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you're saying that Apogee KNOWS people pirate their software     บ
 บ        and is doing nothing to prevent it because Apogee feels that        บ
 บ        stealing is human nature?                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : I'm saying that every computer software programmer knows people     บ
 บ        pirate their software.  There is no such thing as a method of       บ
 บ        protection that can totally prevent your software from being        บ
 บ        stolen.  I'm not saying that Apogee does nothing.  I'm saying that  บ
 บ        you're naive to think you can totally protect your software.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Some companies DO find a way to make sure their software is         บ
 บ        IMPOSSIBLE to pirate on the internet.  They make their games        บ
 บ        ridiculously LARGE.  For example, Phantasmagoria was released on    บ
 บ        seven CDs, will Apogee take that route in the future by making      บ
 บ        games that often take up many CDs?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : I doubt that.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : For example, ALL games that include MacroMedia are IMPOSSIBLE to    บ
 บ        pirate on the internet due to their extensive size, and are thus,   บ
 บ        HARDLY ever pirated.  However, those games that are HARDLY pirated  บ
 บ        do not sell as well as games that ARE pirated.  Why are software    บ
 บ        companies turning to MacroMedia, a form of programming that         บ
 บ        requires HALF the usual programming time and are nearly pirate      บ
 บ        free?                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : If you are inferring that huge CD-Rom games are not pirated, then   บ
 บ        you're wrong.  Haven't you heard of CD-Rom burners?  These things   บ
 บ        are below $1000, and they'll go much lower soon.  The CD-Rom is     บ
 บ        *NOT* protection from copying software anymore, and will be less    บ
 บ        so in the future.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You can copy a huge game from CD to CD, but you cannot upload or    บ
 บ        download them from underground bulletin boards because it would     บ
 บ        take a person about 1 week to download a game on a 33.6kb/s         บ
 บ        US Robotics Modem.  Is that not true?                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : Yeah, but if you think that's the only avenue of piracy, you're     บ
 บ        not seeing everything.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is the main avenue of piracy?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : What do you think it is?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I go over my friend's house and we lend each other SNES games, and  บ
 บ        sometimes PC games too.  I've only copied like 3 games, and I       บ
 บ        guess a lot of my friends also do what I do, so it must add up.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  APG : The internet is the main avenue of trading, and countries outside   บ
 บ        of the United States pose a big problem too.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : The internet?  People pirate on the internet?  So... ya got any     บ
 บ        cool sitez, d00d?                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Method               บ
 บ    Subject  : Couriers on Conquest      Affiliation : COC President        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is Couriers on Conquest?  I assume it's a courier group, but   บ
 บ        what will make it different from all the other courier groups that  บ
 บ        pop up each week?                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : Couriers on Conquest came up from a couple of places.  When DiC     บ
 บ        decided to merge with some no name group, a lot of DiC members did  บ
 บ        not like it so we decided to go run DiC ourselves, but the          บ
 บ        President of DiC didn't like the idea.  Then, a couple local        บ
 บ        friends of mine decided we wanted to run a local courier group for  บ
 บ        the time being; and if it got a good response, then we would take   บ
 บ        it to the NET.  I had a local sysop make up a quick application     บ
 บ        generator and we had a good response of eager couriers,             บ
 บ        programmers, artists, and distribution sites.  We then decided to   บ
 บ        bring it to the NET and so far, we haven't had a bad response.  We  บ
 บ        are different because we aren't out there to get the best name or   บ
 บ        trade the fastest.  We just want to get out there and have some     บ
 บ        fun trying to courier.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Have you experienced any trouble with past DiC members that merged  บ
 บ        with that no name group?  Do any of them hold grudges against you   บ
 บ        or COC?  If so, what have they done?                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : Actually, a day later, the President took a lot of our advice and   บ
 บ        pulled out of the merge, and then DiC fell apart, but now it's      บ
 บ        back under new the new President, Blackened.  I hope they do        บ
 บ        better.  I have never really had a problem with any of the past or  บ
 บ        present DiC members.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What must one do to become a COC member?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : Couriers need to have internet accounts so they can access IRC      บ
 บ        and FTP.  There are really no requirements for distribution sites.  บ
 บ        We are really out to have fun.  If you apply, there's a 99% chance  บ
 บ        you'll get in the group.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Many other groups have proven success by being very selective and   บ
 บ        letting very FEW people in the group.  Why and how do you feel      บ
 บ        that letting in 99% of all applicants will in turn benefit COC?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : I believe in giving everyone a chance to prove themselves, in a     บ
 บ        couple weeks I will cut whoever is slacking.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is COC planning to courier and release in the future since many     บ
 บ        new courier groups do so?                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : We are currently strictly couriering, but may be, this is a big     บ
 บ        may be, if we do succeed in the future, we might release as well    บ
 บ        as courier.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you connect couriering power of a group with how well they can   บ
 บ        release?  The big groups such as RiSC/RTS/MC never release warez.   บ
 บ        Do you think that perhaps a courier group that DOES release might   บ
 บ        not be as good as a courier group that does NOT?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : I see it as, a courier group that does release has more problems    บ
 บ        and is more disorganized because the group needs to worry about     บ
 บ        dupes and fakes.  I think that is why more courier groups go down,  บ
 บ        but courier groups that don't release don't have to worry about     บ
 บ        dupes and fakes and just have to stay organized and courier.  That  บ
 บ        is why I feel that there is a higher chance of COC staying alive    บ
 บ        if we don't release.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Where did you come up with the name COC?  It sounds like a person   บ
 บ        sucking on a cock, isn't that a bad name for the group?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : I know.  I have heard all the little names that COC could stand     บ
 บ        for.  I really don't know.  I thought of conquest and put it all    บ
 บ        together and didn't really think about the initials of the group    บ
 บ        until someone pointed it out to me.  It doesn't really seem to be   บ
 บ        bringing the group down, and I don't think it really matters what   บ
 บ        the name of the group is, as long as we all stay together and well  บ
 บ        organized.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Are there any older courier groups that you model after?            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MTD : Well, there are some courier groups that just go up to get warez    บ
 บ        and then there are REAL courier groups that have made a impression  บ
 บ        on everyone.  I personally like fATE, RiSC, MindCrash, and Legacy.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Legacy is a games group, but anyways, do you feel that your past    บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป

 บ  RCN : Mystic One, what groups are you affiliated with?                    บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ        several high caliber sites for the group.  We had an opportunity    บ
 บ        to make the group into something special.  Unfortunately the        บ
 บ        leadership was not interested in the growth and betterment of the   บ

 บ        long time and he knew that keeping the channel '-i' was a mistake.  บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Raistlindr           บ
 บ    Subject  : fATE                      Affiliation : Ex-fATE Member       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The following is a reinterview with Raistlindr made in order to clear     บ
 บ  some misconceptions :                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why were you kicked out of fATE?                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : I told Anti Derivative when I spoke with him that I was no longer   บ
 บ        in fATE and I thought he understood that.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why did you tell him you were no longer in fATE?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : For a few reasons, 1. The fact that Anti Derivative and god were    บ
 บ        never online to take care of any problems.  2. LeoDLioN is one of   บ
 บ        the most childish and infantile people I know on the net.  3. The   บ
 บ        fact that most of the fATE people were not doing anything.  4. The  บ
 บ        fact that if there was ever a problem, they would just try to kick  บ
 บ        you out of the channel, and did not allow you to defend yourself.   บ
 บ        Those are the main reasons.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : If Anti Derivative and god were not online to take care of          บ
 บ        problems, then who did to help accomplish things?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : In theory, the other seniors did, and that was one of the main      บ
 บ        problems, was the fact that much of it didn't get taken care of.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why do you feel that LeoDLioN is childish and infantile?  He is     บ
 บ        married and has kids.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : That does not matter and is not what I meant.  His attitude and     บ
 บ        how he reacts to other people.  For instance, if he has a problem   บ
 บ        with someone instead of speaking to them rationally or allowing     บ
 บ        them to defend themselves he will just try and kick them out of     บ
 บ        the channel anytime there has been a problem with him.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Has he ever done anything personally to you that would turn you     บ
 บ        off?                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : And when I have stopped the escalation of the problem, he would     บ
 บ        always start up again.  And, yes, he has done a lot to me.  When I  บ
 บ        was still in fATE, he took me off the bots and banned me from       บ
 บ        #fATE because he realized that I was correct and that he could not  บ
 บ        defend his actions, so rather than admit he was wrong or try and    บ
 บ        solve any problems, he just tried to ban me. As long as I was       บ
 บ        still in fATE, as I was, I should not be taken off the bots, much   บ
 บ        less banned from them.  That is just one example of how childish    บ
 บ        he acts.  He did not like the fact that he felt he could question   บ
 บ        what I stated and basically stated I was lying and did not like     บ
 บ        the fact that when he did this, I would defend myself and           บ
 บ        question his actions.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What did you state?                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : Well, I am a very good "warez-encyclopedia".  I know all the files  บ
 บ        and what was out and when, and back then I was not currently in     บ
 บ        DMN (Demolition) and a DMN senior came into the channel and asked   บ
 บ        me directly a question about something DMN was planning on          บ
 บ        releasing and I stated that the program in question was not out as  บ
 บ        of yet.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : To dupe check?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : Yes, to dupe check it.  Then LeoDLioN decided to insert himself in  บ
 บ        the conversation and started ordering me to go log off the NET and  บ
 บ        call Park Central for the files.  I had stated that was not         บ
 บ        necessary as I knew it was not out.  I asked the DMN senior who     บ
 บ        had asked me the question and he stated to me that my answer was    บ
 บ        quite sufficient and the fact that I stated it was enough for him   บ
 บ        to believe it.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So do you belive that LeoDLioN, Anti Derivate, and god were bad     บ
 บ        for fATE, because they either did nothing, or are immature?         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RST : Well, I believe that LeoDLioN is bad for the group and that Anti    บ
 บ        Derivative and god can't be good for it as they are not in enough   บ
 บ        to take care of their duties.  I basically feel that LeoDLioN is    บ
 บ        much too infantile and childish to be more of an asset to a group   บ
 บ        than a hindrance.  For me at least, the main problem was that he    บ
 บ        was very egotistical and felt that his opinions could not be        บ
 บ        questioned, yet still felt that he could question others.  My main  บ
 บ        problem with him was that he inserted himself in a conversation     บ
 บ        that did not involve him and then proceeded to take offense when I  บ
 บ        questioned what he stated because he questioned what I stated.  I   บ
 บ        did not at the time harbor any bad feelings toward god or Anti      บ
 บ        Derivative, but the fact that I tried for over 2 weeks to get in    บ
 บ        touch with one of them to resolve this and neither of them were     บ
 บ        ever in did not help my disposition towards fATE.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
