 บ    Reporter : Raw Toxic                 Interviewee : Majorr               บ
 บ    Subject  : SODOM                     Affiliation : SDM Senior           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is SODOM?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : SODOM is a warez group organized in Russia.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Most of us have never heard of SODOM, how long has SODOM been in    บ
 บ        existence?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : SODOM has been around for a year now, a little less or a little     บ
 บ        more, give or take.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Are warez a big thing in Russia as in comparsion to the United      บ
 บ        States?                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : The warez scene in Russia is about if not equal to the one in the   บ
 บ        United States.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are some of SODOM's goals?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : Our main goal is to monopolize the Russian warez market.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : D0D's slogan is `Warez Bears from Russia'.  Is D0D competition for  บ
 บ        SODOM?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : Actually D0D only has about 3 members who are actually from         บ
 บ        Russia; so their slogan doesn't really fit the entire group.  D0D   บ
 บ        is too large to be a Russian warez group.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is your opinion of the warez scene?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : There's too much worthless crap being released, half of it doesn't  บ
 บ        work, the other half is just useless.  SODOM refuses to courier     บ
 บ        such garbage.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Has the KGB been cutting down on warez in Russia?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : No.  Microsoft has tried to grab some CD retailers, but it was a    บ
 บ        one-time deal.  They failed against the Russian bears!  However,    บ
 บ        there are some laws concerning copyrights in Russia, but they       บ
 บ        don't work at all.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Has SODOM experienced any internal problems?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : No, we don't have many problems for two reasons, we are all in      บ
 บ        SODOM for a common goal, and half of us know each other on a        บ
 บ        personal level.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What do you see in SODOM's future?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : I see that while we are expanding in Russia, we will also grow      บ
 บ        outside of Russia.  We would like to keep more than half of our     บ
 บ        group Russian though.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How does SODOM handle slackers?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : We just kick them out of the group.  It's easy to do it, every      บ
 บ        member in SODOM must contribute something useful.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How is the Russian warez scene different from the American warez    บ
 บ        scene?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : There really aren't any groups in Russia.  SODOM is the only        บ
 บ        serious warez group in Russia.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Has the Russian scene grown considerably due to SODOM?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : Of course not, we aren't the first group in the Russian scene,      บ
 บ        there was DOD before SODOM.  We just want to be the greatest        บ
 บ        Russian group ever.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How are you going to make SODOM the greatest Russian group ever?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : SODOM is going to unite all the guys in Russia who are able to do   บ
 บ        something and we are going to work in that direction.  We have      บ
 บ        many former D0D members joining SODOM so we have a good start.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When you mentioned formerr D0D members, did they give up D0D to     บ
 บ        join SODOM?                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : No, they were kicked out by Jimmy Jamez and SODOM was willing to    บ
 บ        let them in.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How do you say 'warez' in Russian?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MJR : Waresi                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Super Hacker         บ
 บ    Subject  : The Hardened Criminals    Affiliation : THC President        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What sets THC apart from other courier groups?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : Well, there are many things.  One is the name.  As you can see,     บ
 บ        the name is not related nor does it sound like a couriering group.  บ
 บ        It sounds more like bunch of criminals doing illegal activities.    บ
 บ        GUESS WHAT, we are all doing this, and we are all criminals.  The   บ
 บ        main reason why the group is different and set APART from other     บ
 บ        couriering groups is that members in our group are dedicated.  We   บ
 บ        all work in groups and we all have a common goal.  We are here to   บ
 บ        have fun and to help out the warez scene to the best of our         บ
 บ        abilities.  Like we say  "HERO'S COME AND GO, BUT CRIMINALS NEVER   บ
 บ        DIE" SO BANNNNNNNNNG, we are here to stay.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are the minimum requirements for an accepted THC applicant?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : THC looks for dedication, time, and leadership skills in new        บ
 บ        applicants.  We are not like other groups in that we do not ask a   บ
 บ        member to be on IRC 24 hours a day trading.  Everybody has a life   บ
 บ        and we as a group want people to contribute whatever time they can  บ
 บ        and expect only 100% dedication.  If the new member can only        บ
 บ        contribute 5 hours a day trading, then that's cool as long as he    บ
 บ        puts 100% in that 5 hours.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you feel that people might become lazy under that philosphy?     บ
 บ        Is it working for THC so far?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : THC has been working well under our current philosophy.  People     บ
 บ        are not becoming lazy but are becoming more active.  People who     บ
 บ        courier for 5 hours or so are now couriering 10 hours.  I don't     บ
 บ        know how but they are.  They even come up with new ideas of making  บ
 บ        the group more effective, so our philosophy is definitely working.  บ
 บ        We also have members from other groups joining THC because they     บ
 บ        say groups like fATE, RTS, and MOTiV8 require more time.  So the    บ
 บ        facts and answers are right in front of us.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you feel that THC's philosphy will make it one of the BEST       บ
 บ        courier groups in the scene in the not too distant future?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : Yes, I believe that the THC philosophy will make us one of the      บ
 บ        best groups in the near future.  We have just started and we are    บ
 บ        doing well.  I did not expect that but with hard work and           บ
 บ        dedication we are doing really well.  One good thing I really       บ
 บ        enjoyed is that other courier groups don't bug us or do the usual   บ
 บ        CHANNEL TAKEOVERS.  I suppose those things only happen to release   บ
 บ        groups.  Our future plans are not only to accept couriers but to    บ
 บ        accept suppliers as well.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Since THC will be accepting suppliers, will it be releasing under   บ
 บ        a separate name or under THC?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : A branch of THC will release and the other good part will be that   บ
 บ        we can spread our own releases.  Like I said before, we are here    บ
 บ        to contribute toward the warez scene and are giving 100%.  If       บ
 บ        members can supply us with warez, then why not supply and courier   บ
 บ        together.  We can have the best of both worlds.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : THC sounds an awful lot like THG - The Humble Guys.  Did they in    บ
 บ        any way inspire the name THC?  Do members of THC look up to THG as  บ
 บ        models?  I remember memorizing it as an acronym so I could get on   บ
 บ        some lame one node board.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : Well, if you look at the letters THC, you would notice that if you  บ
 บ        flip flop the "T" and the "H", you'd get the name HTC as well; and  บ
 บ        like you said, it can also be flip flopped to form THG.  When I     บ
 บ        first started out in the scene, we were called TGP (Tokyo Ghetto    บ
 บ        Pussy).  We couriered and then changed our name to PWC (Pirate      บ
 บ        Without Cause), but we didn't like it.  The Humble Guys in a way    บ
 บ        did inspire us and so did other groups like PTW, DTC, and HTC.      บ
 บ        We took all the concepts and good parts of all those groups and     บ
 บ        formed THC.  We took all the good parts from each group and made a  บ
 บ        new group with a new look and style.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is THC best at internet or board couriering?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : We are best at board couriering.  The reason for this is that we    บ
 บ        have sysops from many areas.  We asked them to get us one of their  บ
 บ        users from their board who can call internet and get warez off our  บ
 บ        sites.  Using this method, we spread to our boards much faster.     บ
 บ        The users ftp to the sites, they leech 0-1 hour warez and then      บ
 บ        upload it to their assigned board.  The sysops can easily keep      บ
 บ        track of that because the sysop of the boards are all members of    บ
 บ        THC.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is THC's policy on double tagging?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : What is double tagging?                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do THC couriers tag files they help spread?                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SHK : Yes, we put our NFO file in it.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Author  : Demaxxus                                                      บ
 บ    Subject : Anarchist Part Deux                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Tuesday, January 23, 1996                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      On the morning of Tuesday, January 23, 1996, the house of the         บ
 บ  Anarchist (LGC/DMN), was raided.  2 computers were confiscated,           บ
 บ  thousands of dollars in software, and other miscellaneous computer        บ
 บ  hardware.  The Anarchist is facing 5-10 years in jail, a civil suit by    บ
 บ  Microsoft, and possession, distribution, and selling of child             บ
 บ  pornography.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So far, it has taken the police almost a week, and they're still not  บ
 บ  finished going through all his files.  It's also kinda funny, cause       บ
 บ  the police don't have any idea what they're talking about.  Here's a      บ
 บ  quote for you : "We believe it's Microsoft software that he has been      บ
 บ  pir8ing."  Now, I personally wanted to kick that police officer in the    บ
 บ  balls, cause he's a stupid asshole.  The only thing that was on his       บ
 บ  H.D. of Microsoft (pir8'd), was MS Office.  Don't you love when cops      บ
 บ  PRETEND they know what they're talking about.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Monday, January 29, 1996                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In relation to the incident which happened on Brown St. early last    บ
 บ  week, Microsoft and Novell are putting together a task force to come to   บ
 บ  town and investigate.  They will thoroughly search the Anarchist's H.D.   บ
 บ  They will also go through his user log and personally contact all         บ
 บ  members of his BBS (The Shadowlands).  So, if you've called there, and    บ
 บ  used yer real info, beware.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Tuesday, January 30, 1996                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The following is quoted DIRECTLY from The Thunder Bay POST, Vol. 6,       บ
 บ  No. 11 :                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Do you know what your child is doing while he or she is accessing their   บ
 บ  computer?                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  It's a question a lot of moms and dads are asking right now, after the    บ
 บ  RCMP seized child pornography from a home on Brown Street last week.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The pornographic material, according to the RCMP, was just a phone call   บ
 บ  away for thousands of computer users, not only in Thunder Bay, but just   บ
 บ  just about anyone who has a computer and modem.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Where it came from, just what exactly has been seized, and what will      บ
 บ  happen to the operator of a local computer bulletin board is still not    บ
 บ  clear.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Suffice to say the RCMP have a lot of work to do, because so much         บ
 บ  material was seized from the operator of the bulletin board, and 18 year  บ
 บ  old local youth.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  "This material involves young children in sexual situations," says RCMP   บ
 บ  Constable Tom James.  "There are other things we can't reveal because of  บ
 บ  the sensitivity of the investigation.  We don't want to compromise our    บ
 บ  work."                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  What's known so far is that the RCMP executed a search warrant at the     บ
 บ  youth's home last week.  Apparently the parents had no idea what was      บ
 บ  going on and were stunned to learn about the seizure.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  James says none of the material involved local children, and RCMP         บ
 บ  doubt that this material was a small portion of a local "kiddie porn"     บ
 บ  ring.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Yet over the last few days, police have received phone calls reporting    บ
 บ  other illegal material that's floating about the city on other local      บ
 บ  computer bulletin boards.  That's prompted RCMP to pass along advice to   บ
 บ  parents.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  "For those parents who are in doubt, move your child's computer to a      บ
 บ  more open part of the house -- somewhere where parents can keep an eye    บ
 บ  on what their child is doing.  If that's not an option, disconnect the    บ
 บ  modem until you can supervise the on-line session."                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  In the meantime, James says, the RCMP is continuing its investigation.    บ
 บ  Apparently a transmission log, showing exactly who downloaded the         บ
 บ  material, will also be examined.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  At this point, it's still too early to say if charges will be laid.  If   บ
 บ  enough concrete information is received about other child porn or         บ
 บ  illegal material, police will take action.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Miscellaneous Notes                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  reason he had pornography was to get people in our AC to pay for leech    บ
 บ  (they're all porn freaks), and he would therefore be able to make some    บ
 บ  money on the side.  Well.. the Anarchist went too far.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Although I kinda feel sorry for the guy, after all, he's only 18,     บ
 บ  and his whole life is screwed now, and for his family, I don't even want  บ
 บ  to talk about it, he kinda brought this on himself.  It would be ok to    บ
 บ  offer pornography to people 18+ years of age, but, that's not what he     บ
 บ  was doing.  He was offering it to ANYONE that wanted it, and, he was      บ
 บ  offering child pornography, which is VERY illegal, and is the thing that  บ
 บ  is getting him in the most shit.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So Anarchist, if you are somehow reading this, you shouldn't have     บ
 บ  gone so far, but, we're still all behind ya, and good luck.  Latz.        บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Format                                                        บ
 บ    Subject : Bots and Channels                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Keeping your IRC channel in control.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Since I have seen a lot of channel take overs lately, I have decided  บ
 บ  to write this piece on how to keep your channel safe from lame asses who  บ
 บ  are convinced they are hackers simply because they have a copy of         บ
 บ  LinkLooker.  This is aimed toward group channels.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Channel Modes                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      All channels should have the modes '+nst'.  You may want to have a    บ
 บ  bot enforce your chosen channel modes.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Invite only ('+i')                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You may want to have the channel invite only ('+i') as well, but      บ
 บ  this presents a few problems although it can be very beneficial.          บ
 บ  Members, friends, or other people allowed in the channel won't be able    บ
 บ  to get in the channel unless someone in the channel invites them.  This   บ
 บ  can become very frustrating.  However, this problem can be solved by      บ
 บ  putting up a bot that has an invite function.  An alternative to a bot    บ
 บ  is to have a user logged on IRC running a script with functions such as   บ
 บ  '/ctcp <nick> invite'.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Moderated ('+m')                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      While '+m' is implimented, only channel operators, or users who have  บ
 บ  been set with +v can talk in the channel.  This is useful if you want to  บ
 บ  protect the channel from a lot of flooding.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Channel Key ('+k <keyname>')                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If the channel has a channel key set, no one can join the channel     บ
 บ  unless they know the key. eg, the key is 'warez', they have to type       บ
 บ  '/join #chan warez'.  Channel keys are not often used as they are a       บ
 บ  pain.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Channel Limits ('+l <userlimit>')                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Set this only if you want a limited number of people in the channel   บ
 บ  at anyone given time.  This is often used on #WarezX because 300 people   บ
 บ  want to be in it at once.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Setting up someone to keep watch.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Ideally, there should be a maximum of two bots in any channel.  To    บ
 บ  ensure complete protection I suggest running two eggdrops compiled with   บ
 บ  TCL.  The bots should share a common userbase to avoid conflicts.  They   บ
 บ  should have 2 separate server lists too.  This brings me to my next       บ
 บ  point.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Hiding your IRC sentinel from IRC Operators who don't like bots on their  บ
 บ  servers.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      IRC Operators have every right to k-line/ban bots they find, so       บ
 บ  don't complain when your bot is killed by an IRC Operator.  There are     บ
 บ  some tricks however to hide your bot.  It mainly involves changing the    บ
 บ  response from the bot.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  In your eggdrop bot config file add these lines :                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      # response for CTCP VERSION                                           บ
 บ      set ctcp-version "ircII 2.8.2 Linux 1.2.8 :***LiCe(v1.3pl2pre25)      บ
 บ                      By=:SrFrog:=(ircii 2.8: almost there...)"             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      # response for CTCP FINGER                                            บ
 บ      set ctcp-finger "$botnick (${username}@hyper), idle 3 seconds"        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      # response for CTCP USERINFO                                          บ
 บ      set ctcp-userinfo ""                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.  Do NOT give ops to someone unless you are 101% sure they will     บ
 บ          not abuse it.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.  When banning someone, make sure you are doing it on the right     บ
 บ          terms and don't just ban their nick, ban their whole address as   บ
 บ          well!                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.  Do NOT be rude to IRC Operators.  They are there to help you.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4.  Make SURE you revoke anyone's ops if they seem to be abusing it.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      5.  Do NOT develop enemies!  These are the people that will attempt   บ
 บ          to cause chaos.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      6.  Respect other groups, make peace not WAR.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I will gladly offer my services and create bots.  All I ask is that   บ
 บ  you supply me with an account to run it from.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Please send comments to aussie@zonk.geko.net.au.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : ICP                                                           บ
 บ    Subject : Cyrix vs. Intel                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Since the progressive move to the (X)86 series, Intel has maintained  บ
 บ  a stronghold on the CPU market.  After inventing the (X)86 series, Intel  บ
 บ  began moving the market away from the XT/AT shit-o-ramma series.          บ
 บ  However, I have personally felt that Intel's performance has lagged       บ
 บ  recently.  We all remember the wonderful Pentium error the press picked   บ
 บ  up on and widely debated in 1995.  Despite the fact that the error        บ
 บ  wouldn't effect MOST of the computer users, it still troubled me that     บ
 บ  any respectable company would bother to release products without proper   บ
 บ  channels of beta testing.  Such carelessness led me to researching the    บ
 บ  alternative brand extensively.  It seems to be a re-occuring theme for    บ
 บ  respected, profitable, inventive companies to take advantage of their     บ
 บ  fame and fortune by releasing medium quality products at outrageous       บ
 บ  prices.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      One such example, aside from Intel, is US Robotics.  They master      บ
 บ  minded the 14.4 Modem series.  They gained a reputation of being the      บ
 บ  best.  Then what did they do?  They released the USR Sportster 28.8       บ
 บ  v.Everything, one of the most shit-filled modems in the history of        บ
 บ  telecommunications.  Their first few shipments had defective errors,      บ
 บ  crippling its capabilities to even communicate with other modems.  Then,  บ
 บ  as if that wasn't bad enough, several of their latter shipments (when     บ
 บ  the problem was supposed to have been corrected) needed updated software  บ
 บ  to accompany them in order to make the bastards run at 100%.  It is       บ
 บ  these kinds of mistakes that lead me to say, "Well, there goes another    บ
 บ  company...  They're so big now they can make shit products and still      บ
 บ  coherse most people into buying them."  So, I started researching the     บ
 บ  alternatives.  now that I have pissed off several USR lovers out there,   บ
 บ  and believe me, I know the majority of you probably are, let me get back  บ
 บ  to the Intel debate.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      When I went to get a new processor to replace my 486AMD (yes, I went  บ
 บ  against Intel as quickly as I could), I wanted to be really careful.  I   บ
 บ  had heard lots rumors about the competition against the Pentium, namely   บ
 บ  there there really wasn't any.  I think that the general problem is that  บ
 บ  most people just don't know that there is SERIOUS competition to the      บ
 บ  pathetic Intel Pentium chips, namely that of Cyrix.  I looked into AMD    บ
 บ  as well, but their research and moves towards greater products has been   บ
 บ  stagnant in comparison to Cyrix (something very untrue in 486 land).      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Cyrix actually demonstrated the industry's FASTEST Desktop            บ
 บ  processor, the 120 Mhz version of the 6x860 processor family at a trade   บ
 บ  show in Nevada back in November, 1995.  The performance, according to     บ
 บ  desktop PC testing, is expected to rival that of the 166 Mhz Pentium      บ
 บ  processor.  In specified Windows 95 tests, the 120 Mhz Cyrix chip         บ
 บ  conquered all other processors on the CPUMark32 benchmark, which is       บ
 บ  developed to gauge the performance of 32-bit applications under Windows   บ
 บ  95.                                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The amazing features of the Cyrix 6x86 boggle my mind.  Little        บ
 บ  additions such as a 50% die shrink by using all five metal layers of the  บ
 บ  IBM manufacturing process increased production capacity, lowered costs,   บ
 บ  and achieved higher clock speeds.  more complex, important modifications  บ
 บ  of only a few I can FULLY understand account for the wonderful            บ
 บ  performance the rival Pentium CPUs unleash on Intel.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Cyrix claims that the chip is as compatible as the Pentium with       บ
 บ  operating systems and applications.  Apparently the only difference       บ
 บ  between the Intel Pentium and the Cyrix 6x86 CPUs are:                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.  Intel CPUs are more expensive                                     บ
 บ      2.  Intel CPUs are slower when compared to similar Mhz ratings        บ
 บ      3.  Cyrix CPUs are more technologically advanced                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This rivalry could very well have a lot to do with Intel FINALLY      บ
 บ  making dramatic price cuts on the Pentium prices.  Naturally, they        บ
 บ  screwed us as long as they could, but now that Cyrix has begun MASS       บ
 บ  production of their TESTED (unlike Intel) CPUs, Intel has good reason to  บ
 บ  worry that the millions of LAMERS might notice the severe price           บ
 บ  difference of products.  The Cyrix 6x86-100 Mhz CPU cost $450/ea in       บ
 บ  stocks of 1,000, while the rival Intel Pentium 133 Mhz CPU is a much      บ
 บ  higher $520/ea in stocks of 1,000.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Cyrix has pushed their efforts to create a superior CPU ahead of the  บ
 บ  Pentium age.  I believe they have succeeded.  It's time that people rely  บ
 บ  more on their own research when they purchase products such as CPUs and   บ
 บ  other computer related products.  It's important to know how your         บ
 บ  computer functions, but more important to know it functions at its        บ
 บ  highest capabilities for your hard earned dollar.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Author  : ICP                                                           บ
 บ    Subject : fATE's Ancestry                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First off, let me say that this magazine kicks ASS in many respects.  บ
 บ  I'm always busy with couriering, or something of a "warez-e" nature, and  บ
 บ  your production helps me keep up with a lot of the daily politics I miss  บ
 บ  out on in between uploads.  It has especially been of crucial importance  บ
 บ  lately for my main I-Net account was busted and I've had to lay low a     บ
 บ  while...  Busy searching out new servers and the likewise.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      My first concern is with RCN's Review of Courier Teams (RCN #10,      บ
 บ  Articles, Trite).  I happen to be a long-standing fATE member, courier,   บ
 บ  and original co-founder with Calculus, although I openly admit he did     บ
 บ  pull most of the weight in getting the group started.  I believe I have   บ
 บ  held just about every position imaginable as a fATE affiliate at one      บ
 บ  time or another.  iLA (Internet Leeches Anonymous), as it was then        บ
 บ  called, just started my PC scene stay (moving up from stone aged          บ
 บ  C64/128).  Calculus must have seen my integrity and willingness to work,  บ
 บ  for he graciously took me under his wing as a co-head with him and        บ
 บ  SpinDoc.  Since that time I have been President, Senior Council, I-Net    บ
 บ  Head, Site Manager, I-Net Member, and I-Net courier.  most of my          บ
 บ  positional changes came from the unstable management period of fATE       บ
 บ  mixed with my entrance into college.  This is where I would like to get   บ
 บ  into the body of my discussion.  I have laid all this information out,    บ
 บ  NOT TO BRAG, but to present my crudentials within fATE before I spew out  บ
 บ  what input I have to offer.  Anti-Derivative and myself are the only two  บ
 บ  original iLA/fATE members who still exist.  The merger of iLA and TiC     บ
 บ  after all was implemented by Calculus, and in my opinion, saved TiC in a  บ
 บ  way.  At the time, TiC had great board and net support, but lacked the    บ
 บ  effective quality of membership such responsibilities designated.  The    บ
 บ  mix of the two groups is a real strong point in fATE's history.  I        บ
 บ  believe that without the merger, both groups stood an excellent chance    บ
 บ  of withering away into the massive numbers of dead groups.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Not until recently, with the leadership of Anti-Derivate and g0d,     บ
 บ  has fATE seen a solid state of management.  Your review was correct in    บ
 บ  commenting that fATE has (past tense) been having organizational          บ
 บ  problems.  It went through a time period where too many leaders cycled    บ
 บ  in and out of the system.  As a result, they brought in too many friends  บ
 บ  that had no business holding high positions.  But, in reference to the    บ
 บ  present, based on a veteranship I feel I have formed with the term        บ
 บ  "fATE," those days are over for now.  Ever since Anti-Derivative took     บ
 บ  the head position from Red Dog (which I must admit worried me a bit in    บ
 บ  the beginning), and brought g0d in to help out, fATE has been relatively  บ
 บ  well established.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Going into detail on the BLURY conditions the review mentioned        บ
 บ  regarding the absence of Red Dog from fATE... I would like to let you in  บ
 บ  on what really happened as I saw it.  When TiC and iLA merged, Calculus   บ
 บ  and Red DoG sort of shared a top position, above an appointed senior      บ
 บ  council consisting of high members from both groups.  Calculus became     บ
 บ  extremely busy with school and work, so he graciously gave up his reign   บ
 บ  to Red Dog.  This was a very crucial move, and displayed the upmost of    บ
 บ  maturity.  Red Dog's leave from fATE was much the same.  It was           บ
 บ  voluntary, and mature!  He appointed Anti-Derivative to the position,     บ
 บ  dropped himself down in rank, and eventually submerged from the group     บ
 บ  completely.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      On the top of Issue #10, I have read a few interviews of ex-fATE      บ
 บ  members that I found a bit odd.  Ex-members of fATE always complain       บ
 บ  about accessibility of the Senior Members through mail and IRC.  Little   บ
 บ  do they sometimes realize how much time these individuals spend working   บ
 บ  on details they know nothing about.  They aren't on IRC or in fATE's      บ
 บ  respective channels all the time because they take care of a lot of shit  บ
 บ  outside the net.  These guys must spend half their lives going voice to   บ
 บ  people.  It's my humble opinion that many of these ex-fATE members just   บ
 บ  like to gripe, as does most of the scene.  Just ask yourself how many     บ
 บ  negative comments you hear as compared to positive ones out of            บ
 บ  designated "elite" mouths?  If your ratio is at all like the ones I have  บ
 บ  compiled in the past, you'll understand what I am mentioning.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now I'd like to touch up on a bit of the garbage fATE takes from      บ
 บ  other respected members of the scene.  I say respected, because I do      บ
 บ  know many of these individuals from past scene relationships, or just     บ
 บ  because I have dealt with them.  I feel no animosity towards such         บ
 บ  comments, or the people they come from, but I question the judgements     บ
 บ  used in making such remarks.  Yes, there was a time when I would have     บ
 บ  said that fATE was poorly organized, poorly managed, had a lot of         บ
 บ  members that didn't contribute, and needed to be purged, cleaned up, and  บ
 บ  overhauled, but all of those conditions have since been met with          บ
 บ  filtering process after filtering process.  I believe it has left fATE    บ
 บ  as a decent, respectable team of couriers.  I don't doubt that we still   บ
 บ  have our weaknesses, and there is always room for improvement, but that   บ
 บ  is true about every successful group.  I just wish the false accusations  บ
 บ  that still spread throughout channels would halt, or at least be more     บ
 บ  realistic to the truth.  fATE is definitely not the fATE it was two       บ
 บ  months ago, and in no way resembles either iLA or TiC.  I, better than    บ
 บ  most anyone else, have seen the massive changes.  By being dedicated,     บ
 บ  and sticking with fATE (something most people can't figure out, loyalty   บ
 บ  that is) through the good times and down right horrible ones, have seen   บ
 บ  a disasterous, damaged group rise to the couriering level of the best.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I feel many objectionable comments about fATE are justified in        บ
 บ  many respects, but most of the slandering I hear is still based upon a    บ
 บ  version of fATE that died out a long time ago.  I don't feel anyone       บ
 บ  except for Anti-D and myself has any clue as to what really happened to   บ
 บ  fATE in its entirety.  The scene is full of too much spite, rumors, and   บ
 บ  immature infants trying to gain power through takeovers, abuse, and the   บ
 บ  likewise.  I see fATE members accused of this sort of treachory all the   บ
 บ  time, yet, more times than not, I never see, nor hear any proof of        บ
 บ  evidence, just the usual worthless hearsay.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Atomic                                                        บ
 บ    Subject : #M8Leech, a THREAT to #Fatefiles?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Your average IRC user probably hasn't noticed that Motiv8 couriers    บ
 บ  have not setup a new channel on IRC called #M8Leech.  It's supposed to    บ
 บ  be something like #fATEFiles, a channel that is +m (Moderated) and where  บ
 บ  you only offer and leech files, the offered files maybe be no more than   บ
 บ  3 days old.  When you join #M8Leech, though, there aren't half as many    บ
 บ  people as there are in #fATEFiles.  Let's give #M8Leech a chance, though  บ
 บ  because it's just getting started.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I don't know if the idea is to try to divide and conquer (Wasn't it   บ
 บ  Napoleon who said that?!) fATE by beating them on the Internet as well    บ
 บ  as on the boards, maybe that's Motiv8's method of becoming the supreme    บ
 บ  couriering group.  Maybe Motiv8 couriers are trying to become the         บ
 บ  masters of boards AND IRC.  I'm sure that soon enough we will find out    บ
 บ  if Motiv8 is trying to offer something to the scene by providing it with  บ
 บ  a better place to trade in, or if it's trying to use #M8Leech as a        บ
 บ  trick to get bigger than fATE.  Either way, #M8Leech is here now, and it  บ
 บ  looks like it's here to stay.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I was quite happy when I saw Motiv8 starting another channel like     บ
 บ  #fATEFiles because these channels are revolutionizing IRC, making it      บ
 บ  a safe place to spread files fast and easily around the world.  If you    บ
 บ  place a courier in #M8Leech or #fATEFiles and have him offer, you can     บ
 บ  practically be sure that your release will get couriered.  For those of   บ
 บ  us that don't have time to leech off of boards and pump warez to other    บ
 บ  boards, it's very simple just to scan the file offering channels to look  บ
 บ  for anything of interest.  Just beware that to download files from these  บ
 บ  channels, you should be on a ISDN, T1, or better connection to the net    บ
 บ  (or have a provider that has one) because people offering usually set a   บ
 บ  minimum speed that will prevent your average 28.8 from downloading.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Problems arise in these channels when there aren't enough people      บ
 บ  offering and the load of leeches is too high so that so many people want  บ
 บ  to download a specific program that slots fill up and even queues can     บ
 บ  take hours to get through.  I do, however, think that more and more of    บ
 บ  these offer channels will arise, so queues will get smaller and slots     บ
 บ  open slots will be easier to find.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I think the idea of setting up fast offer channels like this one is   บ
 บ  a good one.  On the #WarezX channels, the +m flag is not enforced, so     บ
 บ  the channel is more flooded and that results in higher lag.  Also, the    บ
 บ  files offered in the #WarezX channels are much older than those of        บ
 บ  #fATEFiles and #M8Leech.  Due to the lag in #WarezX, being on more than   บ
 บ  one channel at a time is virtually impossible because so much CRAP is     บ
 บ  coming in from that one channel.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I expect to see many new fast-offer channels like the ones we         บ
 บ  already see, these channels (assuming a speedy connection to the 'net)    บ
 บ  will make IRC THE place to leech from, so look out for these channels     บ
 บ  in the future, they will make IRC a better place for the scene.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Akira 7                                                       บ
 บ    Subject : Game Platforms vs. PC                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The year of 1995 was the year of the video game.  With the launch of  บ
 บ  gaming platforms such as the Sega Saturn and Sony Playstation, the        บ
 บ  quality of home gaming systems has improved by leaps and bounds.  The PC  บ
 บ  may still be the most popular gaming system, but how long will this       บ
 บ  last?  Many critics suggest that the PC will not be the gaming leader     บ
 บ  for much longer.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Sega was the first company to introduce a successfull 32 bit gaming   บ
 บ  system to the market of the United States.  Their system, the Sega        บ
 บ  Saturn, is a very high quality piece of machinery.  With dual CPUs        บ
 บ  running at a total of 28 MHz, the Saturn barely falls short of the Sony   บ
 บ  Playstation in number-crunching power.  The Saturn's graphical engine     บ
 บ  is also slightly inferior to that of the Playstation, but will not make   บ
 บ  a noticable difference.  Sega's main asset is the AM2 design team.        บ
 บ  This game design team is responsible for some of the best arcade hits     บ
 บ  in the country.  Some examples are Daytona USA and Virtua Fighter 2.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Shortly after the Saturn was introduced to the market, Sony dropped   บ
 บ  it's bomb.  The Sony Playstation is perhaps the most technologically      บ
 บ  advanced system on the market today, but their success does not come      บ
 บ  from the 33 MHz CPU.  Sony has experienced incredible 3rd party support   บ
 บ  for their system, and has a large number of games available for it.       บ
 บ  Then number and quality of the games available for the Playstation is     บ
 บ  the main reason for it's success.  With great games like Tekken and       บ
 บ  Destruction Derby, Sony is the leader of today's gaming industry.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Nintendo of America has dominated the market with every new system    บ
 บ  they introduce to the market.  Nintendo's upcoming Ultra 64 will be no    บ
 บ  exception.  When information about the U64 first leaked out in summer     บ
 บ  of 1995, it was rumored to be the "ultimate gaming system."  I couldn't   บ
 บ  have said it better myself.  The Ultra 64 is going to be a true 64 bit    บ
 บ  gaming platform, unlike the Saturn and Playstation which are 32 bit.      บ
 บ  Furthermore, the U64 will have a 128 bit graphics capability, due to      บ
 บ  their custom graphics chip which was engineered by Silicon Graphics       บ
 บ  Inc.  Silicon Graphics is the most well known producer of high end        บ
 บ  graphic workstations in the industry.  The main CPU of the U64 will run   บ
 บ  at a screaming 93.75 MHz (Compared to Sony's 33, this is light speed.)    บ
 บ  and the Rambus system will be running at 500+ MHz.  With upcoming titles  บ
 บ  such as Mario 64 and Killer Instinct, the Ultra 64 will most likely       บ
 บ  dominate the gaming market.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ     And this brings us to the PC.  Where will the PC be in the middle      บ
 บ  of all this activity?  Right where it is now, with interactive CD-ROMs.   บ
 บ  Many critics believe that the PC is getting pushed out of the gaming      บ
 บ  market by systems that are built for gaming, but this is not              บ
 บ  necessarily true.  With new operating sysems such as Windows 95 running   บ
 บ  in 32 bit mode, a higher level of gaming is possible.  Will we be stuck   บ
 บ  hauling around 500mb console-ripped games?  I think not... In the         บ
 บ  future, we will see many more 32 bit games for Win 95 that will be        บ
 บ  comparable to that of the Sony Playstation.  Why, some Playstation        บ
 บ  titles are already for the PC, such as Destruction Derby.  The            บ
 บ  introduction of the P6 chip to the industry will only further the power   บ
 บ  of the 32 bit operating systems of today.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ     Systems like the Saturn and Playstation can generate faster, smoother  บ
 บ  graphics because their components work together much better than in a     บ
 บ  PC.  Some questions to ponder :  Will the introduction of the Ultra 64    บ
 บ  blow away all of the competition?  Will the PC drown in an industry that  บ
 บ  seems to travel too fast for it?  Will Matsushita make powerful PC        บ
 บ  peripherals from his newly bought M2 chip? (Bought from Trip Hawkins for  บ
 บ  $100 million.)  Only the year of 1996 contains the answers.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Krypto                                                        บ
 บ    Subject : School and Warez                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Can School and Warez work together?  For many people in the scene,    บ
 บ  the the answer to this question is "NO."  It is understood that in order  บ
 บ  to achieve greatness at any particular task, one must spend time          บ
 บ  dedicated to it.  This is relevant in both school work and for work       บ
 บ  involved for the scene.  This is where the conflict comes to play.  At    บ
 บ  times, someone may spend hours upon hours couriering warez while not      บ
 บ  spending any attention on their school work.  This usually leads to a     บ
 บ  noticeable drop in school grades.  Even I, myself had to take a leave of  บ
 บ  absence from IRC and the scene in order to bring my grades up.  The drop  บ
 บ  was from a 3.6 to a 1.9 GPA.  This is an all too familiar story for       บ
 บ  many.  One particular example was Superior Force, who in his resignation  บ
 บ  letter complained about how many younger people surpassed him in grades   บ
 บ  and in course level as a direct result of his excessive time spent on     บ
 บ  IRC and in the scene.  He claimed that he had to resign due to a lack of  บ
 บ  good grades.  Others too, such as Rebel Chicken and Manic have stated     บ
 บ  that the scene had dropped their GPA substantially.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                           GPA BEFORE IRC and Warez :                       บ
 บ                           --------------------------                       บ
 บ                             Rebel Chicken - [4.0]                          บ
 บ                                 Hitex - [3.8]                              บ
 บ                                Krypto - [3.6]                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                           GPA AFTER IRC and Warez :                        บ
 บ                           -------------------------                        บ
 บ                                 Hitex - [4.4]                              บ
 บ                             Rebel Chicken - [3.5]                          บ
 บ                                Krypto - [1.9]                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      At this point, we must ask ourselves, "Is there a way to get good     บ
 บ  grades and still be elite?"  This truly is a hard question and            บ
 บ  eventually leads us to efficient time management.  Time management is     บ
 บ  knowing the appropriate time to do things and setting priorities on       บ
 บ  them.  I would recommend to those who are in a similar situations, to do  บ
 บ  their homework and stufies first, then do whatever it is they do in the   บ
 บ  scene later.  The scene will always be here, and USUALLY will not lead    บ
 บ  you to a productive & meaningful education.  Without such education you   บ
 บ  can still do many things such as :                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.  Live in a box for the rest of your life (this means you'd         บ
 บ          probably have to give up your computer eventually).               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.  Go on welfare (you might be able to still retain your computer,   บ
 บ          if you have enough food stamps to sell for some money to pay      บ
 บ          for the electricity bill).                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.  Become a proud member of the local McDonalds staff (seems like a  บ
 บ          fun life, you get all the McNuggets you'd ever want).             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4.  Leech off your parents (when they die, you get to collect the     บ
 บ          life insurance money).                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The point is, DO your homework, study, get good grades, and be        บ
 บ  happy.  Then you can spend all the time you want couriering, supplying,   บ
 บ  or doing whatever else you want.  This all leads us to the next           บ
 บ  question, "When are you going to find time to have sex with your partner  บ
 บ  (this is another topic)?"  Through effective time management, you can     บ
 บ  get good grades and still be elite like me!  And for those of you who     บ
 บ  are getting good grades and have no time management whatsoever, good for  บ
 บ  you!  I'd like to hear how you can do it.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Drapper                                                       บ
 บ    Subject : Running a Site                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, Elmo found me and asked me to write an article about running a  บ
 บ  site.  Since I am a siteop myself, I thought it would be a good idea.     บ
 บ  The first thing that one should consider when starting a site is the      บ
 บ  operating system on which he will run.  If the user has a big hard drive  บ
 บ  (that is, around 4 gigs) then my choice would be to install both a UNIX   บ
 บ  varient and Windows 95.  If the space is smaller then it depends on the   บ
 บ  user.  If he is going to have the machine as a site, and only a site,     บ
 บ  then UNIX is the way to go.  Otherwise, if he thinks he is going to use   บ
 บ  it for his own needs and to test things he gets every day, I would go     บ
 บ  with Windows 95.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Some might think that Windows 95 sucks big time, is very unstable,    บ
 บ  and does not run a good FTP server.  Windows 95, on a 486-100 with 16     บ
 บ  megs and a 1 gig hard drive makes a perfect site!  Just plug in SkyNet    บ
 บ  (CJM's verion of ServU FTP) and you'll have a site up and running in      บ
 บ  less than an hour, while Linux needs a shitload of time and patching.     บ
 บ  Just remember to have a UNIX hacker handy to patch your site or else      บ
 บ  you'll be screwed.  The only advantage I find in Linux is that it has     บ
 บ  better multitasking (but don't forget, no apps to multitask on!) and of   บ
 บ  course the best FTP daemons around that will make a site rock.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are, however, some scripts that are around even for Windows     บ
 บ  95.  There is a SkyNet combo that can have counts of uploads/downloads    บ
 บ  and analytic stats about each user.  The things still missing from        บ
 บ  Windows 95 such as the whois online command, automatic ratios, ZIP        บ
 บ  testing, and stability (you will have a lot of crashes under Windows 95,  บ
 บ  and by the way, anybody that runs Win95 with the Nashville addon should   บ
 บ  remove bwcc.dll from the skynet/servu dir, it causes crashes).            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      After one decides which OS he will put on, he has to find couriers!   บ
 บ  Yeah, a site actually needs couriers and not lamers from #warez5099 to    บ
 บ  upload stuff.  The choices are as follows :  either put as many couriers  บ
 บ  from different groups on and stay a neutral site, or put on couriers      บ
 บ  from one group that will support the site.  The choice is a hard one to   บ
 บ  make and the best is to have both (which is twice as hard of course).     บ
 บ  Finding good couriers and convincing them to support you is the hardest   บ
 บ  part.  this will take much time.  The best thing is to start with a       บ
 บ  small group (but not really lame groups that appear and disappear in      บ
 บ  one or two days!).  Then the group will have some other sites as well     บ
 บ  and will get connections to bigger and bigger sites, and bigger and       บ
 บ  bigger couriers, and will bring them to your site accordingly.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The next step is to get informed about which couriers do a better     บ
 บ  job and are cool people (personal opinion : good couriers with much ego   บ
 บ  = big pile of crap, I bet someone knows who I mean :).  Eventually after  บ
 บ  much time on IRC and many weeks of waiting, the siteop will have found    บ
 บ  at least 1 good courier that will offer good support.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are some general hints on improving a site.  Since I run        บ
 บ  Windows 95, I won't talk about Linux here.  The first thing one should    บ
 บ  do is invoke ratios and start a stats file.  Even though there aren't     บ
 บ  automatic ratio programs for Windows 95, there are some ul/dl counting    บ
 บ  programs that will state ratios as well, so if you are lucky and find     บ
 บ  one of those, you're all set.  Otherwise, you have to do everything by    บ
 บ  hand which is boring, hard, tiring, time consuming, and really stupid.    บ
 บ  With this higher competitive spirit, you'll want to start competitions,   บ
 บ  so the #1 uploader of the week or month gets something (something useful  บ
 บ  in real life, not just for fame which really isn't that useful).          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Finally, a SiteOp should remember the following :                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.  There is always a site that is faster than yours!  That's true    บ
 บ      for everyone and every site.  Even if a site is #1 for a while, soon  บ
 บ      enough someone else will take that position.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.  The site is meant for trading, it's not solely for uploading      บ
 บ      (I like that better), it's for leeching too!  If the siteop thinks    บ
 บ      that he should only have people uploading and not trading as well,    บ
 บ      then he will not be a siteop for very long.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Don't use ridiculous ratios like 1:1!  A good start is 1:4 and if     บ
 บ  you see everything is going fine, move to 1:6.  Sites are up for traders  บ
 บ  to do their job.  One needs to upload and another needs to download.      บ
 บ  There is no problem with that, the site serves people to trade and get    บ
 บ  releases spread.  Also, as a siteop, you should always take care of your  บ
 บ  top 5 couriers.  There might be some time when a courier needs some rest  บ
 บ  or is on vacation, or anything.  That doesn't mean he quit the scene!     บ
 บ  Being inactive for a small period isn't anything bad, so don't nuke       บ
 บ  people hat you know you need!  Leeches need handling as well.  Make sure  บ
 บ  the site has a good ratio of leeches:uploaders (most of the time the      บ
 บ  leeches will be greater, of course).  If you see that leeching goes too   บ
 บ  far then make some warnings and after that start nuking people!           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, that's it folks!  Oh, by the way, running a site ain't as fun   บ
 บ  as it may seem.  After 4 months of running my own site, I'm really bored  บ
 บ  (that doesn't mean my site will go down!).                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Oh, and as a final word, I'd just like to greet some cool dudes out   บ
 บ  there :                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   Prozac ๙ Ionizer ๙ Phrozen Ghost ๙ Night Hawk ๙ Darwin ๙ MaSon ๙ Venix   บ
 บ                                  ๙ HaRy ๙                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       I'd like to diss all couriers who think they're #1 because they're   บ
 บ  moving shit around cables, and who really suck in real life.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the three best game release groups in the scene  บ
 บ  today.  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will  บ
 บ  be!  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but    บ
 บ  you will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let    บ
 บ  me present to you the methods by which I will be reviewing the groups,    บ
 บ  but first, let me name off the groups that will compete in this division  บ
 บ  and state a short reason for why I selected these specific groups to be   บ
 บ  analyzed.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  1. Hybrid - Hybrid has done a great job getting to its ranking in the     บ
 บ              scene today, a relatively short time period in relation to    บ
 บ              its main competition, Razor 1911.  Hybrid pumps awesome       บ
 บ              quality with extreme speed on a regular basis.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  2. Legacy - A newcomer in the game releasing scene, though it has shown   บ
 บ              where it can get in so little time.  Quality hasn't always    บ
 บ              been quite the best, but Legacy tries hard, and doesn't seem  บ
 บ              to be the next one-week group.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  3. Razor 1911 - They're the grandfathers of the games scene.  They've     บ
 บ              had good moments.  They've had bad moments.  They've always   บ
 บ              stuck around, though, and their dedication to the scene is    บ
 บ              definitely something to be proud of.  Oh, and it doesn't      บ
 บ              seem to be the next one-week group <grin>.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now you know who our contestants will be, lets review the criteria    บ
 บ  I will be using for judging releases.  The following is the scoring       บ
 บ  basis I'll be using:                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  -3 - The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   1 - The game worked, but it was a dupe.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   2 - The game worked, but it sucked so bad that nobody would think of     บ
 บ       downloading it.  A proper example would be Legacy's "Bass Fishing    บ
 บ       Classics."                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   3 - Your average release.  Most games will be getting this score.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   4 - Nice release, not budget, many will download and enjoy.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   5 - Damn that was a sweet release!  (I hope Legacy released it, heheh)   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Since we don't play the full game and later find out that something   บ
 บ  didn't work properly, a group may lose points the following week and      บ
 บ  have their release labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amount    บ
 บ  of points).  If the group has released a fix between the two issues,      บ
 บ  we'll give them credit accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a   บ
 บ  3 day period, the program will be rated as if it worked in the first      บ
 บ  place, thus getting the 3 points it lost back and any points it would     บ
 บ  have earned.  If a group releases a fix after the 3 day period has        บ
 บ  expired, it will receive its 3 points back, but get no more.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN will not grant over 3 points to games over 40 disks.  A 40 disk   บ
 บ  release can and will get 5 points if it so deserves, but a 41 disk game,  บ
 บ  I don't care if it's Warcraft III or the Revenge of the Doughnut Boys,    บ
 บ  will not get over 3 points.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.     บ
 บ  If the same program is released under different platforms, it will be     บ
 บ  counted as a single release.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Oh, and you might be asking "How does this differ from Ionizer's      บ
 บ  'The Games Review'?"  Ionizer reviews games for the purpose of            บ
 บ  indicating to us which releases are worth downloading.  We review         บ
 บ  release groups in the only way possible, through their releases.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  So.... MAY THE GAMES BEGIN!                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
