 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the three best util release groups in the scene  บ
 บ  today.  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will  บ
 บ  be!  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but    บ
 บ  you will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let    บ
 บ  me present to you the methods by which I will be reviewing the groups,    บ
 บ  but first, let me name off the groups that will compete in this division  บ
 บ  and state a short reason for why I selected these specific groups to be   บ
 บ  analyzed.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  1. Corporation - They have only been around for a few months, but they    บ
 บ              have definitely shown the scene what they can do.  They have  บ
 บ              pushed through releases at the same speed and quantity as     บ
 บ              other respected groups such as DOD or PWA, and it doesn't     บ
 บ              appear that they're about to stop any time soon.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  2. Drink or Die - Just as their NFO says, these guys really are the       บ
 บ              warez bears from Russia and beyond.  These guys have been     บ
 บ              around for quite a while now and their quality hasn't         บ
 บ              diminished, nor has their quantity.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  3. Pirates with Attitudes - Grandfathers of the Utils scene.  They        บ
 บ              definitely know what they're doing.  Orion's departure        บ
 บ              was a blow to the internal workings of the group, but on the  บ
 บ              outside, they're just as good as they've ever been.  Just as  บ
 บ              any group, they've had their slumps, but their dedication     บ
 บ              has always been one of their biggest assets.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now you know who our contestants will be, lets review the criteria    บ
 บ  I will be using for judging releases.  The following is the scoring       บ
 บ  basis I'll be using :                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  -3 - The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   1 - The util worked, but it was a dupe.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   2 - The util worked, but it sucked so bad that nobody would think of     บ
 บ       downloading it.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   3 - Your average release.  Most utils will be getting this score.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   4 - Nice release, not budget, many will download and enjoy.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   5 - Damn that was a sweet release!                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Since we don't use the entire util and later find out that something  บ
 บ  didn't work properly, a group may lose points the following week and      บ
 บ  have their release labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amount    บ
 บ  of points).  If the group has released a fix between the two issues,      บ
 บ  we'll give them credit accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a   บ
 บ  3 day period, the program will be rated as if it worked in the first      บ
 บ  place, thus getting the 3 points it lost back and any points it would     บ
 บ  have earned.  If a group releases a fix after the 3 day period has        บ
 บ  expired, it will receive its 3 points back, but get no more.  Betas       บ
 บ  may receive no more than 3 points.  If the same program is released       บ
 บ  under different platforms, it will be counted as a single release.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 01/25/96 -> 01/31/96            ณ  บ

 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Need I say anything?  All I'll blurt is that, as I said, quantity is  บ
 บ  important (as PWA showed us) but quality can make the difference.  The    บ
 บ  Corporation had 5 releases this week, where DOD had a mere 3, but DOD's   บ
 บ  quality helped it tie with The Corporation who had some bad fortune on    บ
 บ  their first release of the week (Director Academic v4.0) which required   บ
 บ  a serial number that was released over 3 days past the original release   บ
 บ  date.  If not for that one happening, The Corporation could have beaten   บ
 บ  DOD.  Let's look at the average score per release for each group :        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                         Average Score Per Release :                        บ
 บ                         ---------------------------                        บ
 บ                            Drink or Die - [3.3]                            บ
 บ                       Pirates with Attitudes - [2.8]                       บ
 บ                           The Corporation - [2.0]                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  - After much thought and planning a decision of TGR's future was made.    บ
 บ    This is the last TGR.... to appear alone!  (No, calm down, you'll       บ
 บ    still be able to ge the scene's most reliable source for true,          บ
 บ    unbiased, honest reviews)  It's just going to be found somewhere        บ
 บ    different.  Reality Check Network, now up to their 12th issue, will     บ
 บ    now be the new home for TGR.  Every Sunday, including this one, TGR     บ
 บ    will be found in its own section of RCN (Reviews).  So now, along with  บ
 บ    the best game review, you'll get a packed filled issue of the latest    บ
 บ    group news, interviews, polls  and so much more!  Please don't write    บ
 บ    to me asking what happened to INQ.  INQ is not dead, but due to the     บ
 บ    fact that it is MOST LIKELY that they won't release on a weekly basis,  บ
 บ    TGR would have no appropriate place in their mag.  I wish INQ the best  บ
 บ    of luck in the future, & thank them for carrying TGR in the past.       บ
 บ    (Ok, you're done reading, you can go read the reviews now!)             บ

 บ  - Rating Scale :                                                          บ
 บ              (0-19)/100 = In a nutshell, it sucked!                        บ
 บ             (20-39)/100 = Still crap but slightly better.                  บ
 บ             (40-49)/100 = Possibly worth downloading.                      บ
 บ             (50-69)/100 = Pretty decent game. Might want to check it out.  บ
 บ             (70-79)/100 = Worth the download if you like that type.        บ
 บ             (80-89)/100 = Very good, 9 outta 10 its worth the download.    บ
 บ             (90-99)/100 = Excellent game, a MUST download.                 บ
 บ                 100/100 = HOLY SHIT I'VE NEVER SEEN A BETTER GAME!         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RATINGS are based on the game idea, graphics, sound, playability,         บ
 บ  ingenuity, versatility, and a lot of other words ending in 'ity'.         บ

 บ  soundcard, and then when you load the game up, make sure it's on no       บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Welcome to Dear Entropy!  This is going to be YOUR column that is a   บ
 บ  cross between Dear Abby and Dave Berry.  The most important part of this  บ
 บ  is YOUR participation.  If you have ever had a question about the scene,  บ
 บ  or just a comment, here's the place!  Have you ever wanted to know why    บ
 บ  some people do this or that?  ASK!  We would love to take it to the       บ
 บ  extreme for you and we will be happy to research it!  I hope you have as  บ
 บ  much fun with this as I will!  Remember, this is YOUR column!             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Entropy,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Here's some information about the AOL warez scene and why I used to  บ
 บ  trade warez on AOL :                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       The sheer ease and size of couriering : AOL has long been the        บ
 บ  easiest and fastest way to move warez to a lot of people without a T1 or  บ
 บ  ISDN connections.  Within 5 minutes and a mere 14.4 k baud modem, one     บ
 บ  can mass mail hundreds of 30 meg warez utils and games by simply          บ
 บ  forwarding you warez to 300 or 400 people.  Back when I was on both IRC   บ
 บ  and AOL, I found it much easier to obtain any game or util on AOL than I  บ
 บ  I did on any FTP site or IRC channel.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Except for a few people, no one on AOL has a huge ego trip.  I used  บ
 บ  to be in a warez group on AOL called NmE and END, but the leader, Dawg,   บ
 บ  was one of the fastest dudes I have met.  He uploaded more warez on AOL   บ
 บ  than most couriers in a life time, and was the nicest dude I ever met.    บ
 บ  In fact, find many of the same traits in the AOL warez scene as you do    บ
 บ  in the IRC scene.  There is movement on AOL just as there is on IRC to    บ
 บ  merge the couriering groups and to stop acting like assholes.             บ
 บ  Everything mass mailed or sent on AOL is meant to be free.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      AOLers ain't as dumb as you think.  Recently AOL has taken steps to   บ
 บ  shut down the warez scene on AOL.  Most people have no comprehension of   บ
 บ  the size of the scene.  AOL loses approximately 2-3 million a year due    บ
 บ  AOL piraters.  AOL had implemented a CC number check so that fake CC      บ
 บ  numbers could be used to creat accounts.  Within 5 hours, several         บ
 บ  Windows programers came out with a new hack program which makes accounts  บ
 บ  based on checking, bank and transit members.  Within 2 weeks, AOL         บ
 บ  implemented a procedure that shut down the checking portion of the sign   บ
 บ  up procedures.  Within 1 day, AOLers then proceeded to rely on phishes    บ
 บ  to make sub-accounts from the paying accounts of users.  These accounts   บ
 บ  last until the real user gets his bill <g>.  Now AOLers rely on phishes   บ
 บ  and another proceeder which uses CC number prefixes to get pass the CC    บ
 บ  cc number check.  Recently, the "kewlest" AOLers use OH accounts, which   บ
 บ  give users certain special powers.  Several AOLers have been known to go  บ
 บ  through warez chat rooms and cancel hacked accounts for fun.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Storage of warez on AOL, a lot of people on IRC, more than you would  บ
 บ  expect, store warez on AOL.  AOL has a maximum of 550 mails.  Each mail   บ
 บ  usually contains about 10 megs of space, I have seen 30 megs.  That's at  บ
 บ  least 5,500 megs of warez.  You will find enourmous "banks" of warez on   บ
 บ  AOL.  Some "banks" are available to the public and some are for private   บ
 บ  use.  This is due to the size of couriering and mass mailing and also     บ
 บ  due to the fact that many people don't have the resources for their own   บ
 บ  personal FTP site.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      All right, too much said already about this shit.  Dang, writing      บ
 บ  this much about AOL is making me feel stupid already =]                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Ex-AOLer                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Ex-AOLer,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ     I agree with you completely. AOL is a very powerfull way to reach      บ
 บ   a multitude of user who are to scared or whatever to veture into IRC.    บ
 บ   You are also right that many people that I have met from AOL seem to     บ
 บ   be 100x better then the people on IRC as they seem to now have the       บ
 บ   EGO problem that a lot of us here have to deal with.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  Dear Entropy,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I am writing about the responses about AOL in RCN #11.  I agree with  บ
 บ  both people that responded about AOL.  I've been on AOL for about 1 year  บ
 บ  now.  I know it's not the Internet, but it is THE BEST online service.    บ
 บ  It also has it's advantages to the Internet.  Couriering files are so     บ
 บ  much easier since AOL warez isn't couriered by FTPs ,BBSs, or IRC.  It's  บ
 บ  couriered over attached mail since AOL has no meg limit on their mail     บ
 บ  boxes which makes it simple to get a newly uploaded ware to about 100     บ
 บ  people by just clicking a button.  AOL has a few good warez groups that   บ
 บ  courier warez faster than some internet groups out there.  These groups   บ
 บ  are dedicated to their group and can move files just a few hours after    บ
 บ  their release.  I am in one of those groups, Mystic, and we fill boxes    บ
 บ  up with 0-day ware every day nonstop.  AOL has some more advantages,      บ
 บ  it's cheap, fake accounts are simple to make, killing a lamers account    บ
 บ  is pretty easy, and AOL is made up of 75% idiots (think about what you    บ
 บ  can do with 3 million idiots with CC#'s).   I'm not saying that AOL       บ
 บ  doesn't have it's lamers because that would be bullshit.  I'm just        บ
 บ  sayin that not all AOLers are lame.  There are many former AOLers that    บ
 บ  are in major interne groups such as Razor, Legacy, D0D, and Malice.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Smokey Bebee              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  the die hard IRC'ers and Linux lovers will never admit to Windows or      บ
 บ  almost any GUI program, we all seem to use them and even take advantage   บ
 บ  of some of the perks that it comes with.                                  บ

 บ      Recently on IRC, someone was supposed to be opped on IRC              บ
 บ  automatically by a bot.  When he was not opped he started begging for     บ
 บ  someone to op him.  He kept begging til someone got so fed up that he     บ
 บ  had to op him to shut him up.  This was really unreasonable for someone   บ
 บ  to go to that length just to get a little @ netx to his nick.  I mean,    บ
 บ  what does ops do for you that you can't already do?  Some people show     บ
 บ  that you have power, and most of the people that think that way end up    บ
 บ  kicking, and banning everyone that THEY hate from the channel.  Some      บ
 บ  people think it is a symbol of eliteness, and if someone doesn't have a   บ
 บ  @ by their nick, they're lame.  This little @ shouldn't make you elite    บ
 บ  or lame.  I have been in the net-scene for about 3 to 4 years and I       บ
 บ  don't get @ on all the channels I join.  I know I'm not lame and I        บ
 บ  probably know more about the net-scene than a lot of the ops in the       บ
 บ  channels who kick and ban people.  I know all the people that are just    บ
 บ  starting out in the net-scene and the people that DON'T NEED ops to feel  บ
 บ  eleet will appreciate it if you don't abuse your ops if you do have it.   บ
 บ  My final saying is, please don't beg for ops, because it's annoying, and  บ
 บ  people will get really pissed.                                            บ

 บ     These warez channels in my opinion are good.  When I first found out   บ
 บ  about IRC, I joined these #WarezX to meet people and got too know many    บ
 บ  friends over the many months.  For people in groups like fATE and         บ
 บ  MALiCE, I know of some that used to frequent the channel I was opped in.  บ
 บ  Dr Jekyl would offer and chat in #WarezX a lot during his career as a     บ
 บ  fATE courier.  Cray from HTC is now in RTS and he also comes to hang out  บ
 บ  in #WarezX.  I think these channels are good because it gives you a       บ
 บ  chance to relax from the "stressful" environment of a group.  As far as   บ
 บ  offering goes, I think it's a chance for the couriers to spread their     บ
 บ  warez over a greater "distance" and to help people get their warez        บ
 บ  faster.  As far as why #Warez is better than #Warez1, etc, it is          บ
 บ  probably because the "elite" people, those who have done this for many    บ
 บ  years and have had a great impact on the scene and what not, most of      บ
 บ  these channels probably serve as a relax pit for their "elite" and their  บ
 บ  friends.  However, other channels are very friendly and you can just      บ
 บ  chat about any thing you want when you are bored or if you are a new      บ
 บ  person to the NET and IRC.  It's a wonderful place to start out and to    บ
 บ  make some pals while having fun trading warez.  It's just a plain good    บ
 บ  time.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ

 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Topic For Next Week : Group Monopolies.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Should groups such as RiSC and MALiCE control where and how           บ
 บ  couriering is headed today?  Is there any way we can even control how     บ
 บ  well they are doing?  From what I would say, the last couple of years     บ
 บ  have been RiSC and just that, a rise in superior couriering.  One that    บ
 บ  has dominated the BBS couriering section and will not let anybody else    บ
 บ  enter.  Is this fair?  Should we be allowing smaller groups to try and    บ
 บ  have a chance at couriering?  MALiCE, MindCrash, and fATE have dominated  บ
 บ  NET couriering for almost the past 6 months.  They are on all of the      บ
 บ  best sites and allow nothing to slip through their fingers.  They have    บ
 บ  people on IRC spreading their name to more and more places each day,      บ
 บ  keeping a strong foothold on NET couriering; but do they dominate in      บ
 บ  that they do not give other groups a chance to enter the elite world      บ
 บ  that we live in?  Or should they continue to dominate it and have the     บ
 บ  smaller groups keep working and praying that one day MALiCE will turn     บ
 บ  into TDU-JAM! and quit at their peek?  Some would say that all groups     บ
 บ  work for everything that they attain and I would have to agree with       บ
 บ  them; but would we not work better by working together?  Or does this     บ
 บ  competition really help the scene?  Some people I have talked to think    บ
 บ  that too many people are thinking more about getting the file there       บ
 บ  faster than anybody else but are not being concerned more with if they    บ
 บ  get there 100% error free.  Could the scene better by groups working      บ
 บ  together in taking regions and making sure that everybody has the files   บ
 บ  that the release groups work so hard in releasing?  Is it going so far    บ
 บ  we have threats that some of the biggest and most respected people are    บ
 บ  actually cutting off people from their uploads to be in better spirits    บ
 บ  with the group of their choice?  What do you think?                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
